### Railway Crisis events ###
country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_railway_crisis.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_railway_crisis.1" }
	title = turkestan_railway_crisis.1.t
	desc = turkestan_railway_crisis.1.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_railway_strike

	option = {
		name = turkestan_railway_crisis.1.a
		trigger = {
			RUS = { 
				NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_russia_restored }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_railway_crisis option = TRK_RAILWAY_CRISIS_RUS }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = turkestan_railway_crisis_1_a_tt
		TRK_shokai_pop_mega_decrease_effect = yes
		TRK_decrease_coalition_strength = yes
		add_stability = -0.35
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan_railway_crisis.2
				days = 4
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_railway_crisis.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = turkestan_railway_crisis_1_b_tt
		TRK_erk_pop_medium_effect = yes
		add_political_power = -200
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan_railway_crisis.7
				days = 5
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_railway_crisis.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_railway_crisis.6" }
	title = turkestan_railway_crisis.6.t
	desc = {
		text = turkestan_railway_crisis.6.d
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_country_flag = TRK_shokai_alliance_with_erk }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = turkestan_railway_crisis.6.d2
		trigger = { has_country_flag = TRK_shokai_alliance_with_erk }
	}
		

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_TRK_civil_war

	option = {
		name = turkestan_railway_crisis.6.a		
		trigger = { TRK_has_jadidist_government = yes }
		set_temp_variable = { civ_war_var_change = 10 }
		TRK_shokai_civ_war_change = yes
		TRK_setup_civil_war = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_railway_crisis.6.b
		trigger = { TRK_has_jadidist_government = no }
		set_temp_variable = { civ_war_var_change = 10 }
		TRK_ferghana_civ_war_change = yes
		TRK_setup_civil_war = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_railway_crisis.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_railway_crisis.8" }
	title = turkestan_railway_crisis.8.t
	desc = turkestan_railway_crisis.8.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_TRK_meeting

	option = {
		name = turkestan_railway_crisis.8.a		
		add_stability = -0.15
		RUS = { 
			country_event = { id = turkestan_railway_crisis.18 days = 2 random = 12 }
		}
		TRK_shokai_pop_large_decrease_effect = yes
		TRK_ferghana_pop_large_decrease_effect = yes
		TRK_erk_pop_large_effect = yes
		TRK_mujahideen_pop_large_effect = yes 
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { TRK_ferghana_civ_war_var = -6 }
			add_to_variable = { TRK_shokai_civ_war_var = -6 }
			add_to_variable = { TRK_erk_civ_war_var = 6 }
			add_to_variable = { TRK_mujahideen_civ_war_var = 6 }
		}
		set_temp_variable_to_random = {
			var = TRK_manpower_lost
			min = -2250
			max = -500
		}
		add_manpower = TRK_manpower_lost
	}
}
country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_railway_crisis.9
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_railway_crisis.9" }
	title = turkestan_railway_crisis.9.t
	desc = {
		text = turkestan_railway_crisis.9.d
		trigger = { has_country_flag = RUS_angered_by_strikes }
	}
	desc = {
		text = turkestan_railway_crisis.9.d2
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_angered_by_strikes }
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_railway_strike

	option = {
		name = turkestan_railway_crisis.9.a
		trigger = { 
			has_country_flag = RUS_angered_by_strikes 
			RUS = { 
				NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_russia_restored }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_railway_crisis option = TRK_RAILWAY_CRISIS_IND }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = soviet_russia_restored } }
			TRK_shokai_pop_large_decrease_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			TRK_shokai_pop_medium_decrease_effect = yes
		}
		TRK_decrease_coalition_strength = yes	
		country_event = {
			id = turkestan_railway_crisis.10
			days = 5
		}
		set_country_flag = TRK_railway_diplomacy
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_railway_crisis.9.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_railway_crisis option = TRK_RAILWAY_CRISIS_RUS }
			}
		}
		TRK_shokai_pop_small_effect = yes
		country_event = {
			id = turkestan_railway_crisis.14
			days = 2
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_railway_crisis.11
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_railway_crisis.11" }
	title = turkestan_railway_crisis.11.t
	desc = turkestan_railway_crisis.11.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference1

	option = {
		name = turkestan_railway_crisis.11.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_railway_crisis option = TRK_RAILWAY_CRISIS_RUS }
			}
		}
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { id = turkestan_railway_crisis.12 days = 2 random = 12 }
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_railway_crisis.11.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_railway_crisis option = TRK_RAILWAY_CRISIS_IND }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TRK_benefits_of_tashkent_accords_for_RUS
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { id = turkestan_railway_crisis.13 days = 2 random = 12 }
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = TRK_russian_railways }
					remove_ideas = TRK_russian_railways
				}
				add_ideas = TRK_tashkent_accords
			}			
		}		
	}
}

country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_railway_crisis.13
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_railway_crisis.13" }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_TRK_mustafa_shokai

	option = {
		name = turkestan_railway_crisis.13.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = TRK_russian_railways_can_be_removed
		set_country_flag = central_asia_restored_control_of_railways
		add_ideas = TRK_tashkent_accords
		TRK_decrease_coalition_strength = yes		
		TRK_ferghana_pop_large_decrease_effect = yes
		TRK_shokai_pop_large_decrease_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { turkestan_coalition_stability < 2 } }
				country_event = {
					id = turkestan_railway_crisis.3
					days = 2
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan_railway_crisis.4
				days = 5
				random = 48
			}
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = turkestan_news.1
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan_railway_crisis.4
				days = 5
				random = 48
			}

country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_railway_crisis.19
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_railway_crisis.19" }
	title = turkestan_railway_crisis.19.t
	desc = turkestan_railway_crisis.19.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_TRK_russian_garrison

	option = {
		name = turkestan_railway_crisis.19.a		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_military_access_to = FROM }
			FROM = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = TRK_formal_protest
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_railway_crisis.19.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = embargoed_@FROM }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_political_power < 100
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_military_access_to = FROM }
			FROM = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		effect_tooltip = { embargo_FROM = yes }
		FROM = { 
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan_railway_crisis.20 
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_civil_war.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_civil_war.4" }
	title = turkestan_civil_war.4.t
	desc = turkestan_civil_war.4.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_TRK_civil_war
	
	option = {
		name = turkestan_civil_war.4.a
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				has_socialist_government = yes 
				has_left_democratic_government = yes
			}
			TRK = { NOT = { has_country_flag = TRK_shokai_alliance_with_erk } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_socialist_government = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ALO }
			set_temp_variable = { ush_zhus_pop = 3 }
			every_owned_state = { ALO_ush_zhus_pop = yes }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan_civil_war.7
				days = 2
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_civil_war.4.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_liberal_government = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				tag = UZB 
				UZB_alim_khan_in_power = yes
			}
			UZB_increase_reformists = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = ALO }
			set_temp_variable = { zhanar_pop = 3 }
			every_owned_state = { ALO_zhanar_pop = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { alash_pop = 3 }
			every_owned_state = { ALO_alash_pop = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					popularity = 0.03
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					popularity = 0.03
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan_civil_war.8
				days = 2
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_civil_war.4.c
		trigger = {
			TRK = {
				NOT = { 
					has_country_flag = TRK_madamin_bek_arrested 
					has_country_flag = TRK_madamin_bek_escaped
					has_country_flag = TRK_madamin_bek_escaped_with_mujahideen
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_conservative_government = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				tag = UZB 
				UZB_alim_khan_in_power = yes
			}
			UZB_increase_kushbegi = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}		
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = ALO }
			set_temp_variable = { national_pop = 3 }
			every_owned_state = { ALO_national_pop = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan_civil_war.9
				days = 2
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_civil_war.4.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_dictatorship_government = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				tag = UZB

			}

				days = 2

			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_civil_war.28
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_civil_war.28" }
	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = {
			1209 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		}
	}
	title = turkestan_civil_war.28.t
	desc = {
		text = turkestan_civil_war.28.d
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { TRK_mujahideen_civ_war_var > TRK_erk_civ_war_var }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = turkestan_civil_war.28.d.erk
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { TRK_mujahideen_civ_war_var < TRK_erk_civ_war_var }
				check_variable = { TRK_mujahideen_civ_war_var = TRK_erk_civ_war_var }
			}
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_samarkand_skyline
	
	option = {
		name = turkestan_civil_war.28.a	
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TRK_mujahideen_civ_war_var < TRK_erk_civ_war_var }
					check_variable = { TRK_mujahideen_civ_war_var = TRK_erk_civ_war_var }
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = TRK_samarqand_erk
			set_temp_variable = { civ_war_var_change = 20 }
			TRK_erk_civ_war_change = yes			
			set_temp_variable = { civ_war_var_change = -20 }
			TRK_shokai_civ_war_change = yes			
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { civ_war_var_change = 20 }
			TRK_mujahideen_civ_war_change = yes			
			set_temp_variable = { civ_war_var_change = -20 }
			TRK_shokai_civ_war_change = yes			
		}
		country_event = {
			id = turkestan_civil_war.29
			days = 3
			random = 72
		}
	}
}

			TRK_pop_ruling_medium_decrease_effect = yes
		}

			limit = { has_active_mission = TRK_deal_with_basmachi }
			set_temp_variable = { civ_war_var_change = 7 }
			TRK_mujahideen_civ_war_change = yes
		}

		}

		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = 3500
			producer = ETS
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = support_equipment_1

		}

	}

country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan.233
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan.233" }
	title = turkestan.233.t
	desc = turkestan.233.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_TRK_meeting
	
	option = {
		name = turkestan.233.a
		trigger = {
			TRK_erk_in_power = no
			NOT = { has_war_with = RUS }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		add_political_power = -600		
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_20 = yes
		add_stability = -0.3
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					has_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_1 
					has_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_2 
					has_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_3 
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan.236
				days = 21
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan.233.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_0 }
			TRK_erk_in_power = no
			NOT = { has_war_with = RUS }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_1 }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_1 add_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_0 }
			add_political_power = -400
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan.236
				days = 21
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_2 }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_2 add_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_0 }
			add_political_power = -300
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan.236
				days = 21
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_3 }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_3 add_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_0 }
			add_political_power = -200
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan.236
				days = 21
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_4 }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_4 add_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_1 }
			add_political_power = -100
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_5 }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_5 add_idea = TRK_syr_darya_gold_2 }
		}
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		add_stability = -0.2
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan.233.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}		
		add_political_power = -50
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_socialist_government = no
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TRK_obligations_bad }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan.233.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = TRK_tashkent_accords
				AND = {
					is_in_faction_with = RUS
					RUS = { has_socialist_government = no }
				}
				is_in_faction_with = TRM		
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}		
		add_political_power = -50
		if = {
			limit = { is_ally_with = TRM }
			TRM = { country_event = turkestan.234 }
		}
		else = {
			RUS = { country_event = turkestan.234 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = "If they agree:"

		trigger = { has_idea = TRK_tashkent_accords }
		add_political_power = -120
		remove_ideas = TRK_tashkent_accords
		TRK_pop_ruling_medium_effect = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_jadidist.30
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_jadidist.30" }
	title = turkestan_jadidist.30.t
	desc = turkestan_jadidist.30.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = turkestan_jadidist.30.a
		if = {			
			limit = { tag = ALO }
			set_temp_variable = { alash_pop = 5 }
			every_owned_state = { ALO_alash_pop = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_jadidist.30.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		determine_destination_of_exile_democratic = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:target = { NOT = { tag = XXA } }
			}
			var:target = { 
				country_event = {
					id = turkestan_jadidist.30
					days = 4
					random = 72 
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_qadimist.3" }

	desc = turkestan_qadimist.3.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_TRK_tvo
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = turkestan_qadimist.3.a
		TRK_decrease_tvo_influence = yes
		clr_country_flag = TRK_accepted_tvo_help
		set_country_flag = TRK_konstantin_monstrov_arrested		
		effect_tooltip = {
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 68623 }
				retire = yes
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 68619 }
				retire = yes
			}
		}
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Krestyanskaya Diviziya"
			disband = yes #will refund equipment and manpower
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "TVO Detachment "}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "TVO Detachment"
				disband = yes #will refund equipment and manpower
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 68623 }
				set_nationality = XXA
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 68619 }
				set_nationality = XXA
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = turkestan_qadimist.4
			days = 2
		}
	}
}

			name = "Munawwar Qari Abdurrashidkhan"
			desc = "POLITICS_MUNAWWAR_ANDURRASHIDKHAN_DESC"

			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = jadidism_subtype 
		}
		add_soclib_to_coalition = yes
		add_marlib_to_coalition = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRK_illusion_of_democracy }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TRK_illusion_of_democracy
				add_idea = TRK_illusion_of_democracy_2
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = TRK_illusion_of_democracy_2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				name = TRK_ERK_soclib_party
				long_name = TRK_ERK_soclib_party_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				name = TRK_ERK_soclib_party
				long_name = TRK_ERK_soclib_party_long
			}
			country_event = {
				id = turkestan_socialists.12
				days = 15
				random = 48
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = TRK_erk_alliance_with_jadidists }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = turkestan_socialists.14
					days = 15
					random_days = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_socialists.23
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_socialists.23" }
	title = turkestan_socialists.23.t
	desc = {
		text = turkestan_socialists.23.d
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				check_variable = { TRK_erk_influence_rso > TRK_erk_influence_syn } 
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_path option = TRK_PATH_RADSOC_TORAQULOV }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = turkestan_socialists.23.d2
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				check_variable = { TRK_erk_influence_rso < TRK_erk_influence_syn } 
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_path option = TRK_PATH_SYNDIE }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = turkestan_socialists.23.d3
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				check_variable = { TRK_erk_influence_rso = TRK_erk_influence_syn } 
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_path option = TRK_PATH_RADSOC }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_TRK_erk2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = turkestan_socialists.23.a
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TRK_erk_influence_rso > TRK_erk_influence_syn } 
					AND = {
						is_ai = yes
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_path option = TRK_PATH_RADSOC_TORAQULOV }
					}
				}
			}
			set_politics = { ruling_party = radical_socialist }
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.1 }
			add_ideas = {
				TRK_Nazir_Torekulov_hog_rso
				UZB_Yoldash_Ahunbabayev_for_rso
				TRK_Kadyr_Torekulov_eco_rso
				UZB_Shotemor_Shirinsho_sec_rso
			}
			complete_national_focus = TRK_Socialist_Priority
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TRK_erk_influence_rso < TRK_erk_influence_syn } 
					AND = {
						is_ai = yes
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_path option = TRK_PATH_SYNDIE }
					}
				}
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = 0.1 }
			add_ideas = {
				TRK_Torokul_Dzhanuzakov_hog_syn
				UZB_Usman_Hodzha_for_sde
				UZB_Abdulkodyr_Mukhiddinov_eco_rso
				TRK_Sultonbek_Khojanov_sec_syn
			}
			complete_national_focus = TRK_Junazakov_Leadership
		}
		else = {
			set_politics = { ruling_party = radical_socialist }
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = 0.05 }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Turar Ryskulov"
				desc = "POLITICS_TURAR_RYSKULOV_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/TRK/Portrait_TRK_Turar_Ryskulov.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = left_nationalism_subtype 
			}
			add_ideas = {
				TRK_Turar_Ryskulov_hog_syn
				TRK_Nazir_Torekulov_for_rso
				TRK_Yuldash_Akhunbabayev_eco_rso
				TRK_Sultonbek_Khojanov_sec_syn
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = syndicalist
					name = TRK_syndicalist_party
					long_name = TRK_ERK_syndicalist_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = radical_socialist
					name = TRK_syndicalist_party
					long_name = TRK_ERK_syndicalist_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					name = TRK_syndicalist_party
					long_name = TRK_ERK_syndicalist_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = totalist
					name = TRK_syndicalist_party
					long_name = TRK_ERK_syndicalist_party_long
				}
			}
			complete_national_focus = TRK_Junazakov_Leadership
		}
	}
}

	id = turkestan_socialists.32
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_socialists.32" }
	title = turkestan_socialists.32.t
	desc = turkestan_socialists.32.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = turkestan_socialists.32.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }

			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
			}

				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		else = {
			end_coalition = yes
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = TRK_socialist
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			name = TRK_ERK_syndicalist_party

		}
		add_synd_to_coalition = yes			
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UZB_young_bukhara_radical }			
			hidden_effect = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					name = TRK_ERK_syndicalist_party
					long_name = TRK_ERK_syndicalist_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					name = TRK_ERK_soclib_party
					long_name = TRK_ERK_soclib_party_long
				}
			}
			add_soclib_to_coalition = yes
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			UZB_Usman_Hodzha_hog_sde
			TRK_Turar_Ryskulov_for_syn
			UZB_Abdulkodyr_Mukhiddinov_eco_rso
			TRK_Sultonbek_Khojanov_sec_syn
		}
		CA_recruit_turkestan_erk_leaders = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				name = TRK_ERK_radsoc_party

			}

				long_name = TRK_ERK_syndicalist_party_long
			}			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Turar Ryskulov"
				desc = "POLITICS_TURAR_RYSKULOV_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/TRK/Portrait_TRK_Turar_Ryskulov.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = agrarian_syndicalism_subtype 
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_socialists.36
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_socialists.36" }
	title = turkestan_socialists.36.t
	desc = {
		text = turkestan_socialists.36.d
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { original_tag = KYR }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = turkestan_socialists.36.d2
		trigger = { original_tag = KYR }
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = KYR }
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = TRK }
				TRK = { TRK_erk_in_power = no }
			}
		}
		else = {
			TRK_erk_in_power = yes 
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkestan_socialists.36.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_path option = TRK_PATH_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_path option = TRK_PATH_SYNDIE }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = KYR }						
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Ishaq Bey"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/ETS/Portrait_ETS_Ishaq_Bey.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = national_communism_subtype
			}
			add_tot_to_coalition = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				set_party_name = { 
					ideology = totalist 
					name = KYR_radical_socialist_party
					long_name = KYR_radical_socialist_party_long
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { influence_change = 2 }
			TRK_erk_change_revcom = yes
			add_to_variable = { TRK_erk_influence_sde = 1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.03 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_socialists.36.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRK_path option = TRK_PATH_RADSOC_TORAQULOV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = KYR }						
			add_political_power = -15
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { influence_change = -2 }
			TRK_erk_change_revcom = yes
			add_to_variable = { TRK_erk_influence_sde = -1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = -0.03 }
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = turkestan_socialists.37
					days = 60
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_socialists.37
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_socialists.37" }
	title = turkestan_socialists.37.t
	desc = turkestan_socialists.37.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = turkestan_socialists.37.a
		set_temp_variable = { influence_change = 2 }
		TRK_erk_change_tude = yes
		add_to_variable = { TRK_erk_influence_sde = 1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.03 }
		if = {
			limit = { is_hosting_exile = ETS }
			ETS = {
				add_legitimacy = 10
				set_politics = { ruling_party = syndicalist }
				set_party_name = { 
					ideology = syndicalist
					name = ETS_erk_party
					long_name = ETS_erk_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = { 
					ideology = totalist
					name = ETS_erk_party
					long_name = ETS_erk_party_long
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { ETS_new_socdem = ETS.party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
					divide_temp_variable = { ETS_new_socdem = 2 }

					set_temp_variable = { ETS_new_syndie = ETS.party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
					add_to_temp_variable = { ETS_new_syndie = ETS_new_socdem }

					set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@totalist }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = ETS_new_syndie }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = ETS_new_socdem }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

					add_to_temp_variable = { ETS_new_pataut = sum } #avoid rounding errors

					set_popularities = {
						totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist

						authoritarian_democrat = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat
						paternal_autocrat = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat

		trigger = { original_tag = ETS }
		FROM = { 
			white_peace_with_ROOT = yes 
			effect_tooltip = { turkestan_puppet_ROOT_effect = yes }
			country_event = { id = turkestan_socialists.38 hours = 8 }
		}		
		set_politics = { ruling_party = syndicalist }
		add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = 0.25 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.10 }
		add_tot_to_coalition = yes
		set_party_name = { 
			ideology = syndicalist
			name = ETS_erk_party
			long_name = ETS_erk_party_long
		}
		set_party_name = { 
			ideology = totalist
			name = ETS_erk_party
			long_name = ETS_erk_party_long
		}

		remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister

			ETS_Ehmetjan_Qasim_hog_syn
			ETS_Abdulkerim_Abbas_for_syn
		}

			divide_temp_variable = { ETS_new_socdem = 2 }

			set_temp_variable = { ETS_new_syndie = ETS.party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
			add_to_temp_variable = { ETS_new_syndie = ETS_new_socdem }

			set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@totalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = ETS_new_syndie }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = ETS_new_socdem }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

			add_to_temp_variable = { ETS_new_pataut = sum } #avoid rounding errors

			set_popularities = {
				totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist
				syndicalist = ETS_new_syndie
				radical_socialist = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist
				social_democrat = ETS_new_socdem
				social_liberal = party_popularity_100@social_liberal
				market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal

				national_populist = party_popularity_100@national_populist
			}
		}
		
	}

		}

		trigger = {
			tag = TRK
		}
	}
	

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = turkestan.45.a
		trigger = {
			tag = ALO
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						controls_state = PREV
						tag = FROM
					}
				}
				ROOT = { add_state_core = PREV }
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = FROM
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_CAF
		}				
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan.45.a
		trigger = {
			tag = TRK 
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ALO = { is_ai = yes }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						controls_state = PREV
						tag = ALO
					}
				}
				ROOT = { add_state_core = PREV }
			}

country_event = { #FROM demands ROOT submit
	id = turkestan_events.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_events.1" }
	title = turkestan_events.1.t
	desc = turkestan_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_madamin_bek_and_company

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = turkestan_events.1.a #Yes
		trigger = {
			turkestan_is_potential_government = no
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					turkestan_is_unaligned = yes
					turkestan_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = no
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Aleksandr Dutov" ruling_only = yes }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Timofey Sedelnikov" ruling_only = yes }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Aleksandr Ionov" ruling_only = yes }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail Borodin" ruling_only = yes }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Vladimir Tolstov" ruling_only = yes }
					TRK_monstrov_in_power = yes
					TRK_tvo_in_power = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 99 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				strength_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio < 1 }

			}

				strength_ratio = { tag = ROOT ratio > 1.5 }

				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 199 }

			limit = { RUS_russian_monarch = yes }

			set_autonomy = {
				target = FROM
				autonomous_state = kr_autonomy_russian_imperial_autonomy
				end_wars = no
				end_civil_wars = no
			}
			FROM = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
		}
		else = {
			FROM = { get_current_government_type = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						OR = {
							TRK_tvo_in_power = yes
							TRK_monstrov_in_power = yes
						}
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = TRK_general_governorate
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomous_state = kr_autonomy_russian_general_governorate
					end_wars = no
					end_civil_wars = no
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomous_state = autonomous_territory
					end_wars = no
					end_civil_wars = no
				}			
			}
			FROM = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
		}
	}
}

### NON-SOCIALIST RUSSIA SURRENDER EVENT ###
country_event = { #Stalemate in the CA War
	id = turkestan_events.200
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_events.200" }
	title = turkestan_events.200.t
	desc = turkestan_events.200.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_RUS_army2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = turkestan_events.200.a
		RUS_decrease_ruling_party_pop_large = yes
		set_country_flag = RUS_lost_central_asia_war
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { 
				is_central_asian_tag = yes
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				is_subject = no
			}
			leave_faction = yes
			set_country_flag = @PREV_refused_alliance
		}
		if = {
			limit = { BKN = { has_capitulated = yes } }
			annex_country = { target = BKN }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ALO = { has_capitulated = yes } }
			annex_country = { target = ALO }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { country_exists = ALO }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ALO
					is_owned_by = RUS
				}
				ALO = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		BKN = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }
		ALO = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }
		TRK = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }
		KHI = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }
		KYR = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }
		UZB = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }

		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_central_asia = yes
					NOT = { is_owned_by = RUS }
				}
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = { is_ally_with = RUS }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = RUS }
					remove_core_of = RUS
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = CA_turkestan_victorious
		hidden_effect = { news_event = turkestan_news.52 }
	}
}

	}

country_event = { #Initial event
	id = turkestan_elections.2
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_elections.2" 
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = TRK_negotiations_in_progress
			clr_country_flag = TRK_snap_elections
			clr_country_flag = TRK_pre_elections_flag
			set_variable = { TRK_campaign_ongoing = 0 }
		}
	}
	title = turkestan_elections.2.t
	desc = turkestan_elections.2.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_TRK_qurultai
	trigger = { TRK_erk_in_power = no }

	option = {
		name = turkestan_elections.2.a
		trigger = {
			TRK_jadidist_victory_elections_no_yt = yes
		}		
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberal
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}

news_event = { #
	id = turkestan_news.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event turkestan_news.1" }
	title = turkestan_news.1.t
	desc = turkestan_news.1.d
	
	picture = GFX_news_event_TRK_shokay
	
	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	major = yes	
	show_major = {
		OR = {
			regional_asia_news = yes
			is_neighbor_of = TRK
		}
		NOT = { original_tag = TRK }
	}	

	option = {
		name = turkestan_news.1.a
		trigger = { original_tag = RUS }
	}	
	option = {
		name = turkestan_news.1.b
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				original_tag = KHI
				AND = {
					original_tag = ALO
					ALO = { 
						NOT = { is_subject_of = RUS }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					original_tag = UZB
					UZB = { UZB_has_russian_hegemony = no }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_news.1.c
		trigger = { 
			original_tag = ALO
			ALO = { is_subject_of = RUS }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_news.1.e
		trigger = { 
			original_tag = UZB
			UZB = { UZB_has_russian_hegemony = yes }
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = turkestan_news.1.f
		trigger = { 
			NOT = {
				original_tag = RUS
				original_tag = KHI
				original_tag = ALO
				original_tag = UZB
			}
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = turkestan_news.1.g
		trigger = { 
			NOT = {
				original_tag = RUS
				original_tag = KHI
				original_tag = ALO
				original_tag = UZB
			}
			has_socialist_government = yes
		}
	}	
}
